Tokens ignorados  : WS

Símbolo inicial   : program
Producciones:

  R2: statement_list -> statement_list statement
  R3: statement_list -> statement

  R10: emit_stmt -> KW_EMIT expr SEMICOLON
  R11: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  R12: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_OTHERWISE LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  R13: repeat_stmt -> KW_REPEAT LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_UNTIL LPAREN expr RPAREN SEMICOLON
  R14: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN param_list RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  R15: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE

  R35: expr_mul -> expr_unary
  R36: expr_unary -> NOT expr_unary
  R37: expr_unary -> expr_primary

Reglas (r#):
  accept (S' -> S): program' -> program
  r1: program -> statement_list
  r2: statement_list -> statement_list statement
  r3: statement_list -> statement
  r4: statement -> let_stmt
  r5: statement -> emit_stmt
  r6: statement -> when_stmt
  r7: statement -> repeat_stmt
  r8: statement -> macro_def
  r9: let_stmt -> KW_LET IDENT ASSIGN expr SEMICOLON
  r10: emit_stmt -> KW_EMIT expr SEMICOLON
  r11: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r12: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_OTHERWISE LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r13: repeat_stmt -> KW_REPEAT LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_UNTIL LPAREN expr RPAREN SEMICOLON
  r14: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN param_list RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r15: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r16: param_list -> param_list COMMA IDENT
  r17: param_list -> IDENT
  r18: expr -> expr OR expr_and
  r19: expr -> expr_and
  r20: expr_and -> expr_and AND expr_eq
  r21: expr_and -> expr_eq
  r22: expr_eq -> expr_eq EQ expr_cmp
  r23: expr_eq -> expr_eq NEQ expr_cmp
  r24: expr_eq -> expr_cmp
  r25: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp LT expr_add
  r26: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp GT expr_add
  r27: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp LEQ expr_add
  r28: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp GEQ expr_add
  r29: expr_cmp -> expr_add
  r30: expr_add -> expr_add PLUS expr_mul
  r31: expr_add -> expr_add MINUS expr_mul
  r32: expr_add -> expr_mul
  r33: expr_mul -> expr_mul TIMES expr_unary
  r34: expr_mul -> expr_mul DIV expr_unary
  r35: expr_mul -> expr_unary
  r36: expr_unary -> NOT expr_unary
  r37: expr_unary -> expr_primary
  r38: expr_primary -> INT_LIT
  r39: expr_primary -> FLOAT_LIT
  r40: expr_primary -> STRING_LIT
  r41: expr_primary -> BOOL_LIT
  r42: expr_primary -> IDENT
  r43: expr_primary -> IDENT LPAREN arg_list RPAREN
  r44: expr_primary -> IDENT LPAREN RPAREN
  r45: expr_primary -> LPAREN expr RPAREN
  r46: arg_list -> arg_list COMMA expr
  r47: arg_list -> expr

Sin conflictos: la gramática es compatible con el método elegido.

Reglas (r#):
  accept (S' -> S): program' -> program
  r1: program -> statement_list
  r2: statement_list -> statement_list statement
  r3: statement_list -> statement
  r4: statement -> let_stmt
  r5: statement -> emit_stmt
  r6: statement -> when_stmt
  r7: statement -> repeat_stmt
  r8: statement -> macro_def
  r9: let_stmt -> KW_LET IDENT ASSIGN expr SEMICOLON
  r10: emit_stmt -> KW_EMIT expr SEMICOLON
  r11: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r12: when_stmt -> KW_WHEN LPAREN expr RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_OTHERWISE LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r13: repeat_stmt -> KW_REPEAT LBRACE statement_list RBRACE KW_UNTIL LPAREN expr RPAREN SEMICOLON
  r14: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN param_list RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r15: macro_def -> KW_MACRO IDENT LPAREN RPAREN LBRACE statement_list RBRACE
  r16: param_list -> param_list COMMA IDENT
  r17: param_list -> IDENT
  r18: expr -> expr OR expr_and
  r19: expr -> expr_and
  r20: expr_and -> expr_and AND expr_eq
  r21: expr_and -> expr_eq
  r22: expr_eq -> expr_eq EQ expr_cmp
  r23: expr_eq -> expr_eq NEQ expr_cmp
  r24: expr_eq -> expr_cmp
  r25: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp LT expr_add
  r26: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp GT expr_add
  r27: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp LEQ expr_add
  r28: expr_cmp -> expr_cmp GEQ expr_add
  r29: expr_cmp -> expr_add
  r30: expr_add -> expr_add PLUS expr_mul
  r31: expr_add -> expr_add MINUS expr_mul
  r32: expr_add -> expr_mul
  r33: expr_mul -> expr_mul TIMES expr_unary
  r34: expr_mul -> expr_mul DIV expr_unary
  r35: expr_mul -> expr_unary
  r36: expr_unary -> NOT expr_unary
  r37: expr_unary -> expr_primary
  r38: expr_primary -> INT_LIT
  r39: expr_primary -> FLOAT_LIT
  r40: expr_primary -> STRING_LIT
  r41: expr_primary -> BOOL_LIT
  r42: expr_primary -> IDENT
  r43: expr_primary -> IDENT LPAREN arg_list RPAREN
  r44: expr_primary -> IDENT LPAREN RPAREN
  r45: expr_primary -> LPAREN expr RPAREN
  r46: arg_list -> arg_list COMMA expr
  r47: arg_list -> expr

Sin conflictos: la gramática es compatible con el método elegido.
Parser autónomo generado: build/yapar/pico_lalr_parser.py
